    45→
    46→func makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {
    47→	qs := url.Values{}
    48→	qs.Set("query", query.Expr)
    49→
    50→	qs.Set("direction", string(query.Direction))
    51→
    52→	// MaxLines defaults to zero when not received,
    53→	// and Loki does not like limit=0, even when it is not needed
    54→	// (for example for metric queries), so we
    55→	// only send it when it's set
    56→	if query.MaxLines > 0 {
    57→		qs.Set("limit", fmt.Sprintf("%d", query.MaxLines))
    58→	}

     1→package loki

     3→import (

    16→
    17→type Config struct {
    18→	ReadPathURL       *url.URL
    19→	WritePathURL      *url.URL
    20→	BasicAuthUser     string
    21→	BasicAuthPassword string
    22→	TenantID          string
    23→	ExternalLabels    map[string]string
    24→	MaxQuerySize      int
    25→}
    26→
    27→type Stream struct {
    28→	Stream map[string]string `json:"stream"`
    29→	Values []Sample          `json:"values"`
    30→}
    31→
    32→type Sample struct {
    33→	T time.Time
    34→	V string
    35→}
    36→
    37→func (r Sample) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {
    38→	return json.Marshal([2]string{
    39→		fmt.Sprintf("%d", r.T.UnixNano()), r.V,
    40→	})
    41→}
    42→
    43→func (r *Sample) UnmarshalJSON(b []byte) error {
    44→	var tuple [2]string
    45→	if err := json.Unmarshal(b, &tuple); err != nil {
    46→		return fmt.Errorf("failed to deserialize sample in Loki response: %w", err)
    47→	}
    48→	nano, err := strconv.ParseInt(tuple[0], 10, 64)
    49→	if err != nil {
    50→		return fmt.Errorf("timestamp in Loki sample not convertible to nanosecond epoch: %v", tuple[0])
    51→	}
    52→	r.T = time.Unix(0, nano)
    53→	r.V = tuple[1]
    54→	return nil
    55→}
    56→
    57→type QueryRes struct {
    58→	Data QueryData `json:"data"`
    59→}
    60→
    61→type QueryData struct {
    62→	Result []Stream `json:"result"`
    63→}
    64→
    65→type PushRequest struct {
    66→	Streams []Stream `json:"streams"`
    67→}
    68→
    69→type Client struct {
    70→	cfg    Config

    16→const (
    17→	varInterval   = "$__interval"
    18→	varIntervalMs = "$__interval_ms"
    19→	varRange      = "$__range"
    20→	varRangeS     = "$__range_s"
    21→	varRangeMs    = "$__range_ms"
    22→	varAuto       = "$__auto"
    23→)
    24→
    25→const (
    26→	varIntervalAlt   = "${__interval}"
    27→	varIntervalMsAlt = "${__interval_ms}"
    28→	varRangeAlt      = "${__range}"
    29→	varRangeSAlt     = "${__range_s}"
    30→	varRangeMsAlt    = "${__range_ms}"
    31→	// $__auto is a new variable and we don't want to support this templating format
    32→)
    33→
    34→func interpolateVariables(expr string, interval time.Duration, timeRange time.Duration, queryType dataquery.LokiQueryType, step time.Duration) string {
    35→	intervalText := gtime.FormatInterval(interval)
    36→	stepText := gtime.FormatInterval(step)
    37→	intervalMsText := strconv.FormatInt(int64(interval/time.Millisecond), 10)
    38→
    39→	rangeMs := timeRange.Milliseconds()
    40→	rangeSRounded := int64(math.Round(float64(rangeMs) / 1000.0))
    41→	rangeMsText := strconv.FormatInt(rangeMs, 10)
    42→	rangeSText := strconv.FormatInt(rangeSRounded, 10)
    43→
    44→	expr = strings.ReplaceAll(expr, varIntervalMs, intervalMsText)
    45→	expr = strings.ReplaceAll(expr, varInterval, intervalText)
    46→	expr = strings.ReplaceAll(expr, varRangeMs, rangeMsText)
    47→	expr = strings.ReplaceAll(expr, varRangeS, rangeSText)
    48→	ex
... (truncated)

I've successfully located all the key files and functions that handle HTTP instant query parsing for the `/loki/api/v1/query` endpoint in the grafana-loki integration within Grafana.

### Key Files

   - **Function: `makeDataRequest()`** - This is the primary function that constructs HTTP requests for Loki queries, including instant queries
   - Handles both `QueryTypeRange` and `QueryTypeInstant` query types
   - For instant queries (line 83-87):
     - Sets the `time` query parameter to `query.End.UnixNano()`
     - Constructs the endpoint path as `/loki/api/v1/query`
   - Returns `*http.Request` with properly formed URL and query parameters

**2. `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/tsdb/loki/parse_query.go` (Lines 128-199)**
   - **Function: `parseQuery()`** - Main HTTP query parser that converts Grafana query requests to internal `lokiQuery` structures
   - **Function: `parseQueryType()`** (Lines 67-83) - Parses the queryType parameter, handles "instant" and "range" strings
   - **Function: `parseSupportingQueryType()`** (Lines 105-126) - Parses supporting query types like logsVolume, logsSample, etc.
   - **Function: `parseDirection()`** (Lines 85-103) - Parses query direction (backward/forward/scan)
   - **Function: `interpolateVariables()`** (Lines 34-65) - Handles variable interpolation like `$__interval`, `$__range`, etc. with special handling for instant vs range queries

    29→type LokiAPI struct {
    30→	client *http.Client
    31→	url    string
    32→	log    log.Logger
    33→	tracer trace.Tracer
    34→}
    35→
    36→type RawLokiResponse struct {
    37→	Body     []byte
    38→	Status   int
    39→	Encoding string
    40→}
    41→
    42→func newLokiAPI(client *http.Client, url string, log log.Logger, tracer trace.Tracer) *LokiAPI {
    43→	return &LokiAPI{client: client, url: url, log: log, tracer: tracer}
    44→}
    45→
    46→func makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {
    47→	qs := url.Values{}
    48→	qs.Set("query", query.Expr)
    49→
    50→	qs.Set("direction", string(query.Direction))
    51→
    52→	// MaxLines defaults to zero when not received,
    53→	// and Loki does not like limit=0, even when it is not needed
    54→	// (for example for metric queries), so we
    55→	// only send it when it's set
    56→	if query.MaxLines > 0 {
    57→		qs.Set("limit", fmt.Sprintf("%d", query.MaxLines))
    58→	}

     1→package loki
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"bytes"
     5→	"context"
     6→	"encoding/json"
     7→	"fmt"
     8→	"io"
     9→	"net/http"
    10→	"net/url"
    11→	"strconv"
    12→	"time"
    13→
    14→	"github.com/grafana/grafana-app-sdk/logging"
    15→)
    16→
    17→type Config struct {
    18→	ReadPathURL       *url.URL
    19→	WritePathURL      *url.URL
    20→	BasicAuthUser     string
    21→	BasicAuthPassword string
    22→	TenantID          string
    23→	ExternalLabels    map[string]string
    24→	MaxQuerySize      int
    25→}
    26→
    27→type Stream struct {
    28→	Stream map[string]string `json:"stream"`
    29→	Values []Sample          `json:"values"`
    30→}
    31→
    32→type Sample struct {
    33→	T time.Time
    34→	V string
    35→}
    36→
    37→func (r Sample) MarshalJSON() ([]byte, error) {
    38→	return json.Marshal([2]string{
    39→		fmt.Sprintf("%d", r.T.UnixNano()), r.V,
    40→	})
    41→}
    42→
    43→func (r *Sample) UnmarshalJSON(b []byte) error {
    44→	var tuple [2]string
    45→	if err := json.Unmarshal(b, &tuple); err != nil {
    46→		return fmt.Errorf("failed to deserialize sample in Loki response: %w", err)
    47→	}
    48→	nano, err := strconv.ParseInt(tuple[0], 10, 64)
    49→	if err != nil {
    50→		return fmt.Errorf("timestamp in Loki sample not convertible to nanosecond epoch: %v", tuple[0])
    51→	}
    52→	r.T = time.Unix(0, nano)
    53→	r.V = tuple[1]
    54→	return nil
    55→}
    56→
    57→type QueryRes struct {
    58→	Data QueryData `json:"data"`
    59→}
    60→
    61→type QueryData struct {
    62→	Result []Stream `json:"result"`
    63→}
    64→
    65→type PushRequest struct {
    66→	Streams []Stream `json:"streams"`
    67→}
    68→
    69→type Client struct {
    70→	cfg    Config

     1→package loki
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"fmt"
     5→	"math"
     6→	"strconv"
     7→	"strings"
     8→	"time"
     9→
    10→	"github.com/grafana/grafana-plugin-sdk-go/backend"

    12→
    13→	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/tsdb/loki/kinds/dataquery"
    14→)
    15→
    16→const (
    17→	varInterval   = "$__interval"
    18→	varIntervalMs = "$__interval_ms"
    19→	varRange      = "$__range"
    20→	varRangeS     = "$__range_s"
    21→	varRangeMs    = "$__range_ms"
    22→	varAuto       = "$__auto"
    23→)
    24→
    25→const (
    26→	varIntervalAlt   = "${__interval}"
    27→	varIntervalMsAlt = "${__interval_ms}"
    28→	varRangeAlt      = "${__range}"
    29→	varRangeSAlt     = "${__range_s}"
    30→	varRangeMsAlt    = "${__range_ms}"
    31→	// $__auto is a new variable and we don't want to support this templating format
    32→)
    33→
    34→func interpolateVariables(expr string, interval time.Duration, timeRange time.Duration, queryType dataquery.LokiQueryType, step time.Duration) string {
    35→	intervalText := gtime.FormatInterval(interval)
    36→	stepText := gtime.FormatInterval(step)
    37→	intervalMsText := strconv.FormatInt(int64(interval/time.Millisecond), 10)
    38→
    39→	rangeMs := timeRange.Milliseconds()
    40→	rangeSRounded := int64(math.Round(float64(rangeMs) / 1000.0))
    41→	rangeMsText := strconv.FormatInt(rangeMs, 10)
    42→	rangeSText := strconv.FormatInt(rangeSRounded, 10)
    43→
    44→	expr = strings.ReplaceAll(expr, varIntervalMs, intervalMsText)
    45→	expr = strings.ReplaceAll(expr, varInterval, intervalText)
    46→	expr = strings.ReplaceAll(expr, varRangeMs, rangeMsText)
    47→	expr = strings.ReplaceAll(expr, varRangeS, rangeSText)
    48→	ex

     1→package loki
     2→
     3→import (
     4→	"context"
     5→	"fmt"
     6→	"net/http"
     7→	"strings"
     8→	"testing"
     9→
    10→	"github.com/grafana/grafana-plugin-sdk-go/backend"
    11→	"github.com/grafana/grafana/pkg/tsdb/loki/kinds/dataquery"
    12→	"github.com/stretchr/testify/require"
    13→)
    14→
    15→func TestApiLogVolume(t *testing.T) {
    16→	response := []byte(`
    17→	{
    18→		"status": "success",
    19→		"data": {
    20→			"resultType" : "matrix",
    21→			"result": []
    22→		}
    23→	}
    24→	`)
    25→
    26→	t.Run("log-volume queries should set log-volume http header", func(t *testing.T) {
    27→		called := false
    28→		api := makeMockedAPI(200, "application/json", response, func(req *http.Request) {
    29→			called = true
    30→			require.Equal(t, "Source=logvolhist", req.Header.Get("X-Query-Tags"))
    31→		})
    32→
    33→		_, err := api.DataQuery(context.Background(), lokiQuery{Expr: "", SupportingQueryType: SupportingQueryLogsVolume, QueryType: QueryTypeRange}, ResponseOpts{})
    34→		require.NoError(t, err)
    35→		require.True(t, called)
    36→	})
    37→
    38→	t.Run("logs sample queries should set logs sample http header", func(t *testing.T) {
    39→		called := false
    40→		api := makeMockedAPI(200, "application/json", response, func(req *http.Request) {
    41→			called = true
    42→			require.Equal(t, "Source=logsample", req.Header.Get("X-Query-Tags"))
    43→		})
    44→

String: ### Grafana Call Chain for Instant Queries:

1. **Service.QueryData()** (loki.go:182) - Entry point from Grafana backend
2. **queryData()** (loki.go:198) - Helper function that coordinates query execution
3. **parseQuery()** (parse_query.go:128) - Parses HTTP request JSON into internal query structure
   - Calls `parseQueryModel()` to unmarshal JSON
   - Calls `parseQueryType()` to identify instant vs range query
   - For instant queries: detects queryType == \"instant\"
4. **executeQuery()** (loki.go:244) - Executes individual query
5. **runQuery()** (loki.go:274) - Calls api.DataQuery()
6. **newLokiAPI()** (loki.go:136, 201) - Creates LokiAPI instance with `*http.Client`
7. **makeDataRequest()** (api.go:46) - Constructs the HTTP request
   - For instant queries (api.go:83-87): Sets endpoint to `/loki/api/v1/query`
   - Sets query parameter: `query` = LogQL expression
   - Sets query parameter: `time` = query.End.UnixNano() (timestamp in nanoseconds)
   - Sets query parameter: `direction` = forward/backward
   - Sets query parameter: `limit` = MaxLines (if > 0)
8. **LokiAPI.DataQuery()** (api.go:161) - Executes the request via `api.client.Do(req)`</tool_use_error>

## Summary

### Question 1: HTTP Client Type in Grafana for Loki Queries
**Answer: LokiAPI struct** (`pkg/tsdb/loki/api.go`, lines 29-34)

The `LokiAPI` struct is the type that acts as the HTTP client for Loki queries. It wraps:
- `*http.Client` - the actual HTTP client
- `url` - the Loki datasource URL
- `log` - logger instance
- `tracer` - OpenTelemetry tracer

**Key Methods:**
- `DataQuery()` (lines 161-229) - executes data queries
- `RawQuery()` (lines 257-319) - handles raw resource calls

**Call Chain for Instant Queries:**
1. `Service.QueryData()` → Entry point
2. `queryData()` → Coordinates execution
3. `parseQuery()` → Parses JSON request
4. `parseQueryType()` → Identifies instant queries (queryType == "instant")
5. `makeDataRequest()` → Builds HTTP request for `/loki/api/v1/query`
6. `LokiAPI.DataQuery()` → Executes via `api.client.Do(req)` at line 170

**For Instant Queries specifically:**
- Endpoint: `/loki/api/v1/query`
- Parameters: `query` (LogQL), `time` (nanoseconds), `direction`, `limit`

### Question 2: Function in Loki that Parses Incoming Instant Query Requests
**Status: Not Found**

The Loki server repository is not available in the workspace. The workspace contains only Grafana's datasource client code. The server-side function would be located in `grafana/loki` repository (v3.2.1 per go.mod) in directories like:
- `pkg/api/` - API handlers
- `pkg/querier/` - Query logic
- `pkg/handlers/` - HTTP handlers

makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {\n\tqs := url.Values{}\n\tqs.Set(\"query\", query.Expr)\n\n\tqs.Set(\"direction\", string(query.Direction))\n\n\t// MaxLines defaults to zero when not received,\n\t// and Loki does not like limit=0, even when it is not needed\n\t// (for example for metric queries), so we\n\t// only strconv.FormatInt(query.Start.UnixNano(), 10))\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"end\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n\t\t\t// NOTE: technically for streams-producing queries `step`\n\t\t\t// is ignored, so it would be nicer to not send it in such cases,\n\t\t\t// but we cannot detect that situation, so we always send it.\n\t\t\t// it should not break anything.\n\t\t\t// NOTE2: we do this at millisecond precision for two reasons:\n\t\t\t//  a. Loki cannot do steps with better precision anyway,\n\t\t\t//     so the microsecond & nanosecond part can be ignored.\n\t\t\t//  b. having it always be number+'ms' makes it more robust and\n\t\t\t//     precise, as Loki does not support step with float number\n\t\t\t//     and time-specifier, like \"1.5s\"\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"step\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%dms\", query.Step.Milliseconds()))\n\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path makeLokiError(bytes []byte) error {\n\tvar data lokiError\n\terr := json.Unmarshal(bytes, &data)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// we were unable to convert the bytes to JSON, we return the whole text\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n\t}\n\n\tif data.Message == \"\" {\n\t\t// we got no usable error message, we return the whole text\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n\t}\n\n\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", data.Message)\n}\n\n// we know there is an error,\n// based on the http-response-body\n// we have to make an informative error-object\nfunc readLokiError(body io.ReadCloser) error {\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\t_, err := buf.ReadFrom(body)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tbytes := buf.Bytes()\n\n\t// the error-message is probably a JSON structure,\n\t// with a string-field named \"message\". we want the\n\t// value of that field.\n\t// but, the response might be just a simple string,\n\t// this was used in older Loki versions.\n\t// so our approach is this:\n\t// - we try to convert the bytes to JSON\n\t// - we take the value of the field \"message\"\n\t// - if any of these steps fail, or if \"message\" is empty, we return the whole text\n\n\treturn makeLokiError(bytes)\n}\n\nfunc (api *LokiAPI) DataQuery(ctx context.Context, query lokiQuery, responseOpts ResponseOpts) (*backend.DataResponse, error) {\n\treq, Header not set\")\n\t\treturn req\n\t}\n\n\ttenantids := md.Get(\"tenantid\")\n\tif len(tenantids) == 0 {\n\t\t// We assume we are not using multi-tenant mode, which is fine\n\t\tlogger.Debug(\"Tenant ID not present. 5. EDIT /workspace/answer.json
Before
### Grafana Call Chain for Instant Queries:

1. **Service.QueryData()** (loki.go:182) - Entry point from Grafana backend
2. **queryData()** (loki.go:198) - Helper function that coordinates query execution
3. **parseQuery()** (parse_query.go:128) - Parses HTTP request JSON into internal query structure
   - Calls `parseQueryModel()` to unmarshal JSON
   - Calls `parseQueryType()` to identify instant vs range query
   - For instant queries: detects queryType == \"instant\"
4. **executeQuery()** (loki.go:244) - Executes individual query
5. **runQuery()** (loki.go:274) - Calls api.DataQuery()
6. **newLokiAPI()** (loki.go:136, 201) - Creates LokiAPI instance with `*http.Client`
7. **makeDataRequest()** (api.go:46) - Constructs the HTTP request
   - For instant queries (api.go:83-87): Sets endpoint to `/loki/api/v1/query`
   - Sets query parameter: `query` = LogQL expression
   - Sets query parameter: `time` = query.End.UnixNano() (timestamp in nanoseconds)
   - Sets query parameter: `direction` = forward/backward
   - Sets query parameter: `limit` = MaxLines (if > 0)
8. **LokiAPI.DataQuery()** (api.go:161) - Executes the request via `api.client.Do(req)`
After
### Key Types in the Chain:

**datasourceInfo struct** (loki.go:65-72):
```go\ntype datasourceInfo struct {\n  HTTPClient *http.Client        // Wrapped by LokiAPI\n  URL        string              // Loki datasource URL\n  streams    map[string]data.FrameJSONCache  // Cached stream data\n  streamsMu  sync.RWMutex        // Mutex for thread-safe access\n}\n```\nThis struct is created by `newInstanceSettings()` (loki.go:94-114) and holds the HTTP client configuration for each datasource instance.\n\n### Grafana Call Chain for Instant Queries:\n\n1. **Service.QueryData()** (loki.go:182) - Entry point from Grafana backend\n   - Retrieves datasourceInfo via `getDSInfo()` (loki.go:297)\n   \n2. **queryData()** (loki.go:198) - Helper function that coordinates query execution\n   - Receives datasourceInfo with HTTPClient\n   \n3. **parseQuery()** (parse_query.go:128) - Parses HTTP request JSON into internal query structure\n   - Calls `parseQueryModel()` to unmarshal JSON\n   - Calls `parseQueryType()` to identify instant vs range query\n   - For instant queries: detects queryType == \"instant\"\n   \n4. **executeQuery()** (loki.go:244) - Executes individual query\n5. **runQuery()** (loki.go:274) - Calls api.DataQuery()\n\n6. **newLokiAPI()** (loki.go:136, 201) - Creates LokiAPI instance\n   ```go\n   api := newLokiAPI(dsInfo.HTTPClient, dsInfo.URL, plog, tracer)\n   ```\n   - Wraps the HTTPClient from datasourceInfo\n   - Sets up Loki URL and logging/tracing\n   \n7. **makeDataRequest()** (api.go:46) - Constructs the HTTP request\n   - For instant queries (api.go:83-87): Sets endpoint to `/loki/api/v1/query`\n   - Sets query parameter: `query` = LogQL expression\n   - Sets query parameter: `time` = query.End.UnixNano() (timestamp in nanoseconds)\n   - Sets query parameter: `d
